\sssc{include/tuple.hpp}
\label{tuple-list}
Line~12--751：
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
namespace mystd {

template <class First, class... Rest> struct _first_type {
  using type = First;
};

template <class... Ts> using _first_type_t = typename _first_type<Ts...>::type;

template <typename T> struct _is_tuple : std::false_type {};

template <typename T> inline constexpr bool _is_tuple_v = _is_tuple<T>::value;

template <std::size_t I, class... Types> struct _tuple_impl;

template <std::size_t I> struct _tuple_impl<I> {
  template <std::size_t J> using element_type = void;

  constexpr _tuple_impl() {}
  constexpr _tuple_impl(const _tuple_impl &) noexcept {}
  constexpr _tuple_impl(_tuple_impl &&) noexcept {}

  template <class Alloc>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &) noexcept {}

  template <class Alloc>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &,
                        const _tuple_impl &) noexcept {}

  template <class Alloc>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &,
                        _tuple_impl &&) noexcept {}

  constexpr _tuple_impl &operator=(const _tuple_impl &) noexcept {
    return *this;
  }

  constexpr _tuple_impl &operator=(_tuple_impl &&) noexcept { return *this; }

  void swap(_tuple_impl &other) {}
};

template <std::size_t I, class Head, class... Tail>
struct _tuple_impl<I, Head, Tail...> : public _tuple_impl<I + 1, Tail...> {
  using base = _tuple_impl<I + 1, Tail...>;
  Head head;

  template <std::size_t J>
  using element_type =
      std::conditional_t<J == I, Head, typename base::template element_type<J>>;

  constexpr _tuple_impl()
    requires(std::is_default_constructible_v<Head> &&
             (std::is_default_constructible_v<Tail> && ...))
      : base(), head() {}

  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<const Head &, Head> ||
            (!std::is_convertible_v<const Tail &, Tail> ||
             ...))) constexpr _tuple_impl(const Head &arg, const Tail &...args)
    requires std::is_constructible_v<Head, const Head &> &&
                 (std::is_constructible_v<Tail, const Tail &> && ...)
      : base(args...), head(arg) {}

  template <class UHead, class... UTail>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<UHead, Head> ||
            (!std::is_convertible_v<UTail, Tail> ||
             ...))) constexpr _tuple_impl(UHead &&arg, UTail &&...args)
    requires(sizeof...(Tail) == sizeof...(UTail)) &&
                std::is_constructible_v<Head, UHead> &&
                (std::is_constructible_v<Tail, UTail> && ...)
      : base(std::forward<UTail>(args)...), head(std::forward<UHead>(arg)) {}

  template <typename Alloc>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &alloc)
    requires std::is_default_constructible_v<Head> &&
                 (std::is_default_constructible_v<Tail> && ...)
      : base(mystd::allocator_arg, alloc), head() {}

  template <typename Alloc>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &alloc,
                        const Head &arg, const Tail &...args)
    requires std::is_constructible_v<Head, const Head &> &&
                 (std::is_constructible_v<Tail, const Tail &> && ...)
      : base(mystd::allocator_arg, alloc, args...), head(arg) {}

  template <typename Alloc, class UHead, class... UTail>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &alloc, UHead &&arg,
                        UTail &&...args)
    requires(sizeof...(Tail) == sizeof...(UTail)) &&
                std::is_constructible_v<Head, UHead> &&
                (std::is_constructible_v<Tail, UTail> && ...)
      : base(mystd::allocator_arg, alloc, std::forward<UTail>(args)...),
        head(std::forward<UHead>(arg)) {}

  constexpr _tuple_impl(const _tuple_impl &other)
    requires(std::is_copy_constructible_v<Head> &&
             std::is_copy_constructible_v<base>)
      : base(static_cast<const base &>(other)), head(other.head) {}

  constexpr _tuple_impl(_tuple_impl &&other)
    requires(std::is_move_constructible_v<Head> &&
             std::is_move_constructible_v<base>)
      : base(std::move(static_cast<base &>(other))),
        head(std::move(other.head)) {}

  template <class Alloc>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &alloc,
                        const _tuple_impl &other)
    requires(std::is_copy_constructible_v<Head> &&
             std::is_copy_constructible_v<base>)
      : base(mystd::allocator_arg, alloc, static_cast<const base &>(other)),
        head(other.head) {}

  template <class Alloc>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &alloc,
                        _tuple_impl &&other)
    requires(std::is_move_constructible_v<Head> &&
             std::is_move_constructible_v<base>)
      : base(mystd::allocator_arg, alloc,
             std::move(static_cast<base &>(other))),
        head(std::move(other.head)) {}

  template <class Alloc, class... UTypes>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &alloc,
                        const _tuple_impl<I, UTypes...> &other)
    requires(sizeof...(Tail) + 1 == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
                std::is_constructible_v<Head,
                                        const typename std::remove_cvref_t<
                                            _first_type_t<UTypes...>> &> &&
                std::is_constructible_v<
                    base, const typename _tuple_impl<I, UTypes...>::base &>
      : base(mystd::allocator_arg, alloc,
             static_cast<const typename _tuple_impl<I, UTypes...>::base &>(
                 other)),
        head(other.head) {}

  template <class Alloc, class... UTypes>
  constexpr _tuple_impl(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &alloc,
                        _tuple_impl<I, UTypes...> &&other)
    requires(sizeof...(Tail) + 1 == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
                std::is_constructible_v<
                    Head, std::remove_cvref_t<_first_type_t<UTypes...>>> &&
                std::is_constructible_v<
                    base, typename _tuple_impl<I, UTypes...>::base>
      : base(mystd::allocator_arg, alloc,
             std::move(static_cast<typename _tuple_impl<I, UTypes...>::base &>(
                 other))),
        head(std::move(other.head)) {}

  constexpr _tuple_impl &operator=(const _tuple_impl &other)
    requires std::is_copy_assignable_v<Head> && std::is_copy_assignable_v<base>
  {
    head = other.head;
    base::operator=(other);
    return *this;
  }

  constexpr _tuple_impl &operator=(_tuple_impl &&other) noexcept(
      std::is_nothrow_move_assignable_v<Head> &&
      std::is_nothrow_move_assignable_v<base>)
    requires(std::is_move_assignable_v<Head> && std::is_move_assignable_v<base>)
  {
    head = std::move(other.head);
    base::operator=(std::move(other));
    return *this;
  }

  template <class UHead, class... UTail>
  constexpr _tuple_impl &operator=(const _tuple_impl<I, UHead, UTail...> &other)
    requires(sizeof...(Tail) == sizeof...(UTail)) &&
            std::is_assignable_v<Head &, const UHead &> &&
            std::is_assignable_v<base &, const _tuple_impl<I + 1, UTail...> &>
  {
    head = other.head;
    base::operator=(static_cast<const _tuple_impl<I + 1, UTail...> &>(other));
    return *this;
  }

  template <class UHead, class... UTail>
  constexpr _tuple_impl &
  operator=(_tuple_impl<I, UHead, UTail...> &&other) noexcept(
      std::is_nothrow_assignable_v<Head &, UHead &&> &&
      std::is_nothrow_assignable_v<base &, _tuple_impl<I + 1, UTail...> &&>)
    requires(sizeof...(Tail) == sizeof...(UTail)) &&
            std::is_assignable_v<Head &, UHead &&> &&
            std::is_assignable_v<base &, _tuple_impl<I + 1, UTail...> &&>
  {
    head = std::move(other.head);
    base::operator=(
        static_cast<_tuple_impl<I + 1, UTail...> &&>(std::move(other)));
    return *this;
  }

  constexpr void swap(_tuple_impl &other) noexcept(
      std::is_nothrow_swappable_v<Head> &&
      noexcept(std::declval<base &>().swap(std::declval<base &>()))) {
    mystd::swap(head, other.head);
    static_cast<base &>(*this).swap(static_cast<base &>(other));
  }

  template <std::size_t J>
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() &
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return (head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<base &>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }

  template <std::size_t J>
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() const &
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return (head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<const base &>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }

  template <std::size_t J>
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() &&
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return std::move(head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<base &&>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }

  template <std::size_t J>
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() const &&
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return std::move(head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<const base &&>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }
};

template <class... Types> class tuple {
public:
  _tuple_impl<0, Types...> _impl;

  constexpr tuple()
    requires(std::is_default_constructible_v<Types> && ...)
      : _impl() {}

  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<const Types &, Types> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(const Types &...args)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) >= 1) &&
            (std::is_copy_constructible_v<Types> && ...)
      : _impl(args...) {}

  template <class... UTypes>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<UTypes, Types> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(UTypes &&...args)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) >= 1) &&
            (sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes> && ...) &&
            (sizeof...(Types) > 1 ||
             !mystd::_is_tuple_v<
                 std::remove_cvref_t<_first_type_t<UTypes...>>>) &&
            (sizeof...(Types) > 3 ||
             !std::is_same_v<std::remove_cvref_t<_first_type_t<UTypes...>>,
                             mystd::allocator_arg_t> ||
             std::is_same_v<_first_type_t<Types...>, mystd::allocator_arg_t>)
      : _impl(std::forward<UTypes>(args)...) {}

  template <class... UTypes>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<Types, const UTypes &> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(const tuple<UTypes...> &other)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_constructible_v<Types, const UTypes &> && ...) &&
            (!(sizeof...(Types) == 1 &&
               ((std::is_convertible_v<UTypes, Types> || ...) ||
                (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes> || ...) ||
                (std::is_same_v<Types, UTypes> || ...))))
      : _impl(other._impl) {}

  template <class... UTypes>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<Types, UTypes &&> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(tuple<UTypes...> &&other)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes &&> && ...) &&
            (!(sizeof...(Types) == 1 &&
               ((std::is_convertible_v<UTypes, Types> || ...) ||
                (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes> || ...) ||
                (std::is_same_v<Types, UTypes> || ...))))
      : _impl(std::move(other._impl)) {}

  template <class U1, class U2>
  explicit(
      (!std::is_convertible_v<
           U1, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>> ||
       !std::is_convertible_v<
           U2, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<
                   1>>)) constexpr tuple(const std::pair<U1, U2> &p)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == 2) &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>,
                U1> &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<1>, U2>
      : _impl(p.first, p.second) {}

  template <class U1, class U2>
  explicit((
      !std::is_convertible_v<
          U1 &&, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>> ||
      !std::is_convertible_v<
          U2 &&, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<
                     1>>)) constexpr tuple(std::pair<U1, U2> &&p)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == 2) &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>,
                U1 &&> &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<1>,
                U2 &&>
      : _impl(std::move(p.first), std::move(p.second)) {}

  tuple(const tuple &other) : _impl(other._impl) {}

  tuple(tuple &&other) : _impl(std::move(other._impl)) {}

  template <class Alloc>
  constexpr tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a)
    requires(std::is_default_constructible_v<Types> && ...)
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a) {}

  template <class Alloc>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<const Types &, Types> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a,
                                  const Types &...args)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) >= 1) &&
            (std::is_copy_constructible_v<Types> && ...)
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, args...) {}

  template <class Alloc, class... UTypes>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<UTypes, Types> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a,
                                  UTypes &&...args)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) >= 1) &&
            (sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes> && ...) &&
            (sizeof...(Types) > 1 ||
             !mystd::_is_tuple_v<std::remove_cvref_t<_first_type_t<UTypes...>>>)
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, std::forward<UTypes>(args)...) {}

  template <class Alloc, class... UTypes>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<Types, const UTypes &> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a,
                                  const tuple<UTypes...> &other)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_constructible_v<Types, const UTypes &> && ...) &&
            (!(sizeof...(Types) == 1 &&
               ((std::is_convertible_v<UTypes, Types> || ...) ||
                (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes> || ...) ||
                (std::is_same_v<Types, UTypes> || ...))))
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, other._impl) {}

  template <class Alloc, class... UTypes>
  explicit((!std::is_convertible_v<Types, UTypes &&> ||
            ...)) constexpr tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a,
                                  tuple<UTypes...> &&other)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes &&> && ...) &&
            (!(sizeof...(Types) == 1 &&
               ((std::is_convertible_v<UTypes, Types> || ...) ||
                (std::is_constructible_v<Types, UTypes> || ...) ||
                (std::is_same_v<Types, UTypes> || ...))))
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, std::move(other._impl)) {}

  template <class Alloc, class U1, class U2>
  explicit(
      (!std::is_convertible_v<
           U1, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>> ||
       !std::is_convertible_v<
           U2, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<
                   1>>)) constexpr tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a,
                                         const std::pair<U1, U2> &p)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == 2) &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>,
                U1> &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<1>, U2>
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, p.first, p.second) {}

  template <class Alloc, class U1, class U2>
  explicit((
      !std::is_convertible_v<
          U1 &&, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>> ||
      !std::is_convertible_v<
          U2 &&, typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<
                     1>>)) constexpr tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t,
                                           const Alloc &a,
                                           std::pair<U1, U2> &&p)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == 2) &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<0>,
                U1 &&> &&
            std::is_constructible_v<
                typename _tuple_impl<0, Types...>::template element_type<1>,
                U2 &&>
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, std::move(p.first),
              std::move(p.second)) {}

  template <class Alloc>
  tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a, const tuple &other)
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, other._impl) {}

  template <class Alloc>
  tuple(mystd::allocator_arg_t, const Alloc &a, tuple &&other)
      : _impl(mystd::allocator_arg, a, std::move(other._impl)) {}

  constexpr tuple &operator=(const tuple &other)
    requires(std::is_copy_assignable_v<Types> && ...)
  {
    _impl = other._impl;
    return *this;
  }

  constexpr tuple &operator=(tuple &&other) noexcept(
      (std::is_nothrow_move_assignable_v<Types> && ...))
    requires(std::is_move_assignable_v<Types> && ...)
  {
    _impl = std::move(other._impl);
    return *this;
  }

  template <class... UTypes>
  constexpr tuple &operator=(const tuple<UTypes...> &other)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_assignable_v<Types &, const UTypes &> && ...)
  {
    _impl = other._impl;
    return *this;
  }

  template <class... UTypes>
  constexpr tuple &operator=(tuple<UTypes...> &&other)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == sizeof...(UTypes)) &&
            (std::is_assignable_v<Types &, UTypes &&> && ...)
  {
    _impl = std::move(other._impl);
    return *this;
  }

  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() & noexcept {
    return _impl.template get<J>();
  }

  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() && noexcept {
    return std::move(_impl).template get<J>();
  }

  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() const & noexcept {
    return _impl.template get<J>();
  }

  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() const && noexcept {
    return std::move(_impl).template get<J>();
  }

  template <class E1, class E2>
  constexpr tuple &operator=(const std::pair<E1, E2> &p)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == 2) &&
            std::is_assignable_v<decltype(this -> get<0>()), const E1 &> &&
            std::is_assignable_v<decltype(this->get<1>()), const E2 &>
  {
    this->get<0>() = p.first;
    this->get<1>() = p.second;
    return *this;
  }

  template <class E1, class E2>
  constexpr tuple &operator=(std::pair<E1, E2> &&p) noexcept(
      std::is_nothrow_assignable_v<decltype(this->get<0>()), E1 &&> &&
      std::is_nothrow_assignable_v<decltype(this->get<1>()), E2 &&>)
    requires(sizeof...(Types) == 2) &&
            std::is_assignable_v<decltype(this -> get<0>()), E1 &&> &&
            std::is_assignable_v<decltype(this->get<1>()), E2 &&>
  {
    this->get<0>() = std::move(p.first);
    this->get<1>() = std::move(p.second);
    return *this;
  }

  constexpr void swap(tuple &other) noexcept(
      noexcept((std::is_nothrow_swappable_v<Types> && ...))) {
    _impl.swap(other._impl);
  }

private:
  template <std::size_t... I>
  static constexpr bool tuple_equal_impl(const tuple &a, const tuple &b,
                                         std::index_sequence<I...>) {
    return ((a.get<I>() == b.get<I>()) && ...);
  }

public:
  friend constexpr bool operator==(const tuple &a, const tuple &b) {
    return tuple_equal_impl(a, b, std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(Types)>{});
  }

private:
  template <std::size_t... I>
  static constexpr auto tuple_three_way_impl(const tuple &a, const tuple &b,
                                             std::index_sequence<I...>)
      -> std::common_comparison_category_t<decltype(a.get<I>() <=>
                                                    b.get<I>())...> {
    using result_t = std::common_comparison_category_t<decltype(a.get<I>() <=>
                                                                b.get<I>())...>;
    result_t result = result_t::equal;
    ((result = (result != 0 ? result : (a.get<I>() <=> b.get<I>()))), ...);
    return result;
  }

public:
  friend constexpr auto operator<=>(const tuple &a, const tuple &b) {
    return tuple_three_way_impl(a, b,
                                std::make_index_sequence<sizeof...(Types)>{});
  }
};

template <> class tuple<> {
public:
  constexpr tuple() noexcept = default;

  constexpr tuple(const tuple &) noexcept = default;
  constexpr tuple(tuple &&) noexcept = default;

  constexpr tuple &operator=(const tuple &) noexcept = default;
  constexpr tuple &operator=(tuple &&) noexcept = default;

  constexpr void swap(tuple &) noexcept {}

  friend constexpr bool operator==(const tuple &, const tuple &) noexcept {
    return true;
  }

  friend constexpr auto operator<=>(const tuple &, const tuple &) noexcept {
    return std::strong_ordering::equal;
  }
};

template <class... UTypes> tuple(UTypes...) -> tuple<UTypes...>;

template <class T1, class T2> tuple(std::pair<T1, T2>) -> tuple<T1, T2>;

template <class Alloc, class... UTypes>
tuple(std::allocator_arg_t, Alloc, UTypes...) -> tuple<UTypes...>;

template <class Alloc, class T1, class T2>
tuple(std::allocator_arg_t, Alloc, std::pair<T1, T2>) -> tuple<T1, T2>;

template <class Alloc, class... UTypes>
tuple(std::allocator_arg_t, Alloc, tuple<UTypes...>) -> tuple<UTypes...>;

template <typename... Ts>
struct _is_tuple<mystd::tuple<Ts...>> : std::true_type {};

template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept {
  return t.template get<I>();
}

template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept {
  return std::move(t).template get<I>();
}

template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept {
  return t.template get<I>();
}

template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept {
  return std::move(t).template get<I>();
}

template <class T, class... Types> struct _count_of_type;

template <class T>
struct _count_of_type<T> : std::integral_constant<std::size_t, 0> {};

template <class T, class Head, class... Tail>
struct _count_of_type<T, Head, Tail...>
    : std::integral_constant<std::size_t,
                             (std::is_same_v<T, Head> ? 1 : 0) +
                                 _count_of_type<T, Tail...>::value> {};

template <class T, class... Types>
inline constexpr std::size_t _count_of_type_v =
    _count_of_type<T, Types...>::value;

template <class T, class... Types> struct _index_of_type;

template <class T, class... Tail>
struct _index_of_type<T, T, Tail...> : std::integral_constant<std::size_t, 0> {
};

template <class T, class Head, class... Tail>
struct _index_of_type<T, Head, Tail...>
    : std::integral_constant<std::size_t,
                             1 + _index_of_type<T, Tail...>::value> {};

template <class T> struct _index_of_type<T> {};

template <class T, class... Types>
inline constexpr std::size_t _index_of_type_v =
    _index_of_type<T, Types...>::value;

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(mystd::tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(t);
}

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(mystd::tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(std::move(t));
}

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const mystd::tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(t);
}

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const mystd::tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(std::move(t));
}

template <class... Types> constexpr auto make_tuple(Types &&...args) {
  return mystd::tuple<typename std::decay<Types>::type...>(
      std::forward<Types>(args)...);
}

template <class... Types>
constexpr mystd::tuple<Types &...> tie(Types &...args) noexcept {
  return mystd::tuple<Types &...>(args...);
}

template <class... Types>
constexpr tuple<Types &&...> forward_as_tuple(Types &&...args) noexcept {
  return tuple<Types &&...>(std::forward<Types>(args)...);
}

template <class... Tuples> struct _tuple_cat_type;

template <> struct _tuple_cat_type<> {
  using type = mystd::tuple<>;
};

template <class... Ts> struct _tuple_cat_type<mystd::tuple<Ts...>> {
  using type = mystd::tuple<Ts...>;
};

template <class... Ts1, class... Ts2, class... Rest>
struct _tuple_cat_type<mystd::tuple<Ts1...>, mystd::tuple<Ts2...>, Rest...> {
  using type =
      typename _tuple_cat_type<mystd::tuple<Ts1..., Ts2...>, Rest...>::type;
};

template <class... Tuples>
using _tuple_cat_type_t = typename _tuple_cat_type<Tuples...>::type;

template <class T1, class T2, std::size_t... I1, std::size_t... I2>
constexpr auto _tuple_cat_two_impl(T1 &&t1, T2 &&t2, std::index_sequence<I1...>,
                                   std::index_sequence<I2...>) {
  return mystd::tuple{mystd::get<I1>(std::forward<T1>(t1))...,
                      mystd::get<I2>(std::forward<T2>(t2))...};
}

template <class T1, class T2> constexpr auto _tuple_cat_two(T1 &&t1, T2 &&t2) {
  return _tuple_cat_two_impl(
      std::forward<T1>(t1), std::forward<T2>(t2),
      std::make_index_sequence<
          std::tuple_size<std::remove_cvref_t<T1>>::value>{},
      std::make_index_sequence<
          std::tuple_size<std::remove_cvref_t<T2>>::value>{});
}

template <class T> constexpr auto _tuple_cat_impl(T &&t) {
  return std::forward<T>(t);
}

template <class T1, class T2, class... Rest>
constexpr auto _tuple_cat_impl(T1 &&t1, T2 &&t2, Rest &&...rest) {
  auto first = _tuple_cat_two(std::forward<T1>(t1), std::forward<T2>(t2));
  return _tuple_cat_impl(std::move(first), std::forward<Rest>(rest)...);
}

template <class... Tuples> constexpr auto tuple_cat(Tuples &&...tpls) {
  return _tuple_cat_impl(std::forward<Tuples>(tpls)...);
}

template <class... Types>
constexpr void
swap(mystd::tuple<Types...> &lhs,
     mystd::tuple<Types...> &rhs) noexcept(noexcept(lhs.swap(rhs))) {
  lhs.swap(rhs);
}

template <class... Types, class Alloc>
struct uses_allocator<std::tuple<Types...>, Alloc> : std::true_type {};

} // namespace mystd

namespace std {

template <class... Types>
struct tuple_size<mystd::tuple<Types...>>
    : std::integral_constant<std::size_t, sizeof...(Types)> {};

template <class Head, class... Tail>
struct tuple_element<0, mystd::tuple<Head, Tail...>> {
  using type = Head;
};

template <std::size_t I, class Head, class... Tail>
struct tuple_element<I, mystd::tuple<Head, Tail...>>
    : tuple_element<I - 1, mystd::tuple<Tail...>> {};

} // namespace std
\end{lstlisting}

\ssc{2-C-4-3 polymorphism 相關的 class 或 function 間的對應關係}
\label{2-C-4-3}
承上，本專題未使用 runtime polymorphism，而是廣泛使用 compile-time polymorphism。

具體個案的對應關係可參考前兩章所列之內容中 template arguments 等處得知，下文將針對其各類型說明設計理念與核心概念。
\sssc{Substitution Failure Is Not An Error (SFINAE)}
\label{sfinae}
SFINAE is a compile-time technique in template programming. If substituting template parameters results in an invalid type or expression, the compiler silently ignores that overload instead of producing an error. This mechanism enables selective template instantiation and overload resolution.
\sssc{Concepts}
\label{concepts}
C++20 introduces \textbf{concepts}, which allow explicit constraints on template parameters in a readable and expressive way. Concepts replace some uses of SFINAE with clearer syntax. Key benefits include:
\begin{itemize}
    \item Clear compile-time diagnostics.
    \item Explicit template constraints.
    \item Improved code readability and maintainability.
\end{itemize}
In my STL implementation, concepts are heavily used to determine the appropriate overload or \texttt{if constexpr} branch. This technique enables optimizations for trivially copyable types, contiguous iterators, allocator traits-based optimization, etc.

Many examples are demonstrated in \textbf{2-B-1-2 指標成員處理} 中的 \hyperref[vector-list]{\textbf{include/vector.hpp}} and described in its \hyperref[vector-describe]{\textbf{描述}}.

Some other examples in \verb|include/algorithm-copy.hpp| is described as follows. The file provides three basic data transfer algorithms: \verb|copy|, \verb|copy_if|, and \verb|copy_backward|, mimicking the interface design of C++20 \verb|<algorithm>|. The copy function family demonstrates the polymorphism programming techniques, particularly conceptual parameter constraints and conditional optimization strategies.

I utilize concepts for constraints, such as \verb|std::input_iterator|, \verb|std::weakly_incrementable|, \verb|std::bidirectional_iterator|, and \verb|std::indirectly_writable| in the definition, and
\verb|std::contiguous_iterator| and \verb|std::is_trivially_copyable_v| for specialized acceleration.

In \verb|copy| algorithms, I use \verb|std::memcpy| when possible and element-wise assignment only when necessary, as demonstrated below (line~7--32)
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template <std::input_iterator InputIt, std::weakly_incrementable OutputIt>
  requires std::indirectly_writable<OutputIt, std::iter_value_t<InputIt>>
constexpr OutputIt copy(InputIt first, InputIt last, OutputIt d_first) {
  if constexpr (std::contiguous_iterator<InputIt> &&
                std::contiguous_iterator<OutputIt> &&
                std::is_trivially_copyable_v<
                    typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type> &&
                std::is_same_v<
                    typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type,
                    typename std::iterator_traits<OutputIt>::value_type>) {
    if (first == last)
      return d_first;
    const auto *src = std::to_address(first);
    const auto *src_end = std::to_address(last);
    auto *dest = std::to_address(d_first);
    const std::size_t count = (src_end - src) * sizeof(*src);
    std::memcpy(dest, src, count);
    return d_first + (last - first);
  }
  while (first != last) {
    *d_first = *first;
    ++first;
    ++d_first;
  }
  return d_first;
}
\end{lstlisting}

Similarly, in \verb|copy_backward| algorithm, \verb|std::memmove| is used when possible, as demonstrated below (line~49--73)
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template <std::bidirectional_iterator BidirIt1,
          std::bidirectional_iterator BidirIt2>
constexpr BidirIt2 copy_backward(BidirIt1 first, BidirIt1 last,
                                 BidirIt2 d_last) {
  using ValueType1 = typename std::iterator_traits<BidirIt1>::value_type;
  using ValueType2 = typename std::iterator_traits<BidirIt2>::value_type;
  if constexpr (std::contiguous_iterator<BidirIt1> &&
                std::contiguous_iterator<BidirIt2> &&
                std::is_trivially_copyable_v<ValueType1> &&
                std::is_same_v<ValueType1, ValueType2>) {
    auto n = last - first;
    if (n > 0) {
      std::memmove(std::addressof(*d_last) - n, std::addressof(*first),
                   n * sizeof(ValueType1));
    }
    return d_last - n;
  } else {
    while (first != last) {
      --last;
      --d_last;
      *d_last = *last;
    }
    return d_last;
  }
}
\end{lstlisting}
\sssc{Class Template Argument Deduction (CTAD)}
\label{ctad}
C++17 introduced \textbf{Class Template Argument Deduction (CTAD)}, allowing the compiler to deduce template parameters from constructor arguments. STL containers provide \textbf{deduction guides} to assist this process, which are also implemented in my library to improve usability.

Take \verb|mystd::priority_queue| for example, the CTADs are as follows:\\
(\verb|include/priority_queue.hpp| line~212--242)
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template <class Comp, class Container>
priority_queue(Comp, Container)
    -> priority_queue<typename Container::value_type, Container, Comp>;

template <
    std::input_iterator InputIt,
    class Comp = std::less<typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type>,
    class Container =
        mystd::vector<typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type>>
priority_queue(InputIt, InputIt, Comp = Comp(), Container = Container())
    -> priority_queue<typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type,
                      Container, Comp>;

template <class Comp, class Container, class Alloc>
priority_queue(Comp, Container, Alloc)
    -> priority_queue<typename Container::value_type, Container, Comp>;

template <std::input_iterator InputIt, class Alloc>
priority_queue(InputIt, InputIt, Alloc) -> priority_queue<
    typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type,
    mystd::vector<typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type>,
    std::less<typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type>>;

template <std::input_iterator InputIt, class Comp, class Alloc>
priority_queue(InputIt, InputIt, Comp, Alloc) -> priority_queue<
    typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type,
    mystd::vector<typename std::iterator_traits<InputIt>::value_type>, Comp>;

template <std::input_iterator InputIt, class Comp, class Container, class Alloc>
priority_queue(InputIt, InputIt, Comp, Container, Alloc)
    -> priority_queue<typename Container::value_type, Container, Comp>;
\end{lstlisting}
\sssc{Empty Base Optimization (EBO)}
\label{ebo}
In C++, an empty class normally has size 1 to ensure unique addresses. EBO is a compiler optimization that allows empty base classes to occupy no additional storage when used as a base.

In my implementation, Empty Base Optimization (EBO) is applied within \verb|_tuple_impl| in \verb|include/tuple.hpp|, which underlies the internal recursive inheritance mechanism of \verb|tuple|. The design begins with an empty base class for the recursion terminator: (line~26)
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template <std::size_t I> struct _tuple_impl<I>
\end{lstlisting}
Then, the recursive inheritance is implemented as follows: (line~53--55)
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template <std::size_t I, class Head, class... Tail>
struct _tuple_impl<I, Head, Tail...> : public _tuple_impl<I + 1, Tail...> {
  using base = _tuple_impl<I + 1, Tail...>;
\end{lstlisting}
\sssc{Template Compile-Time Recursion}
\label{recursion}
Templates can perform computation at compile time using recursion:
\begin{itemize}
    \item Each template instantiation computes one step of the recursion.
    \item Recursion terminates at a base case specialization.
    \item Computation occurs entirely at compile time, producing constant expressions.
\end{itemize}
This technique is used extensively in \verb|include/tuple.hpp| to implement functions that access elements, indices, element types, etc. An example is demonstrated by the \hyperref[get]{\textbf{get functions in include/tuple.hpp}} section. Some more examples are listed in \textbf{2-C-4-1 polymorphism 宣告} 的 \hyperref[tuple-list]{\textbf{include/tuple.hpp}}.
\sssc{std::declval template}
\label{declval}
\texttt{std::declval<T>()} defined in \texttt{<utility>} is a template intended exclusively for use in unevaluated contexts (such as within \texttt{decltype}, \texttt{sizeof}, or SFINAE expressions). It provides a fictional value of type \texttt{T} or \texttt{T\&} without requiring that the type be constructible. This enables compile-time type deduction even for non-instantiable or non-default-constructible types.

\texttt{std::declval} is indispensable in implementing traits and SFINAE-based detection idioms. One example is as follows: (\verb|include/tuple.hpp| line~204--209)
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
  constexpr void swap(_tuple_impl &other) noexcept(
      std::is_nothrow_swappable_v<Head> &&
      noexcept(std::declval<base &>().swap(std::declval<base &>()))) {
    mystd::swap(head, other.head);
    static_cast<base &>(*this).swap(static_cast<base &>(other));
  }
\end{lstlisting}
\sssc{Ref-Qualified Member Functions}
\label{ref-qualified}
C++11 introduced \textbf{ref-qualified} member functions. These allow a class to distinguish overloads based on whether the object is an lvalue (\texttt{\&}) or an rvalue (\texttt{\&\&}).

This mechanism is widely used in the member functions overloads in STL to control move semantics and perfect forwarding. An example is demonstrated by the \hyperref[get]{\textbf{get functions in include/tuple.hpp}} section. Some more examples are listed in \textbf{2-C-4-1 polymorphism 宣告} 的 \hyperref[tuple-list]{\textbf{include/tuple.hpp}}.
\sssc{decltype}
\label{decltype}
\texttt{decltype} is a compile-time operator that deduces the declared type of an expression without performing the expression's evaluation. Unlike \verb|auto|, which uses assignment-like deduction rules, \texttt{decltype} preserves the exact type, including references and cv-qualifiers.

Given an expression \verb|e|, the type deduced by \texttt{decltype(e)} depends on the
expression category.
\begin{itemize}
    \item If \verb|e| is a unparenthesized id-expression naming a variable, then \texttt{decltype(e)} yields the declared type of the variable. Note that a parenthesized one is a lvalue expression.
    \item If \verb|e| is an \textbf{lvalue} expression, \texttt{decltype(e)} yields \verb|T&|.
    \item If \verb|e| is an \textbf{xvalue}, \texttt{decltype(e)} yields \verb|T&&|.
    \item If \verb|e| is a \textbf{prvalue}, \texttt{decltype(e)} yields \verb|T|.
\end{itemize}

\verb|decltype(auto)| preserves the exact type of the initializer.

\texttt{decltype} is crucial in producing type traits or meta-functions in template metaprogramming in many templates in my implementation, and \verb|decltype(auto)| is also used together with perfect forwarding and template overloads in my implementation. An example is demonstrated by the \hyperref[get]{\textbf{get functions in include/tuple.hpp}} section. Some more examples are listed in \textbf{2-C-4-1 polymorphism 宣告} 的 \hyperref[tuple-list]{\textbf{include/tuple.hpp}}.
\sssc{Curiously Recurring Template Pattern (CRTP)}
The Curiously Recurring Template Pattern (CRTP) is a C++ idiom in which a class Derived inherits from a class template Base that takes Derived itself as a template parameter.

CRTP allows classes to achieve polymorphic behavior at compile time, combining interface abstraction, code reuse, and high performance. It is particularly suitable when runtime overhead of virtual functions is undesirable or when the set of derived classes is fixed at compile time.
\sssc{get functions in include/tuple.hpp}
\bit
\item Member functions of
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template <std::size_t I, class Head, class... Tail>
struct _tuple_impl<I, Head, Tail...>
\end{lstlisting}
: \texttt{get<J>} member functions provide compile-time element access and are overloaded for all value categories: lvalue, const lvalue, rvalue, and const rvalue. The implementation uses \texttt{if constexpr} to check whether the requested index $J$ matches the current index $I$. This design allows efficient compile-time recursion to navigate tuple elements while preserving proper value category semantics without runtime overhead.

Line~211--253:
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() &
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return (head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<base &>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }

  template <std::size_t J>
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() const &
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return (head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<const base &>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }

  template <std::size_t J>
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() &&
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return std::move(head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<base &&>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }

  template <std::size_t J>
  constexpr decltype(auto) get() const &&
    requires(J >= I && J <= I + sizeof...(Tail))
  {
    if constexpr (I == J) {
      return std::move(head);
    } else {
      return static_cast<const base &&>(*this).template get<J>();
    }
  }
\end{lstlisting}
\item Member functions of \verb|template <class... Types> class tuple|: The \texttt{tuple} class delegates all element access to its internal \texttt{\_tuple\_impl} member \texttt{\_impl}. All public \texttt{get<J>} member functions forward the access while preserving constness and value categories.

Line~466--480:
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() & noexcept {
    return _impl.template get<J>();
  }

  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() && noexcept {
    return std::move(_impl).template get<J>();
  }

  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() const & noexcept {
    return _impl.template get<J>();
  }

  template <std::size_t J> constexpr decltype(auto) get() const && noexcept {
    return std::move(_impl).template get<J>();
  }
\end{lstlisting}
\item Non-member functions and helpers: Non-member \texttt{get<I>} functions allow element access using ADL and provide interface for tuples complying with C++20 standard. Compile-time type traits, \texttt{\_count\_of\_type} and \texttt{\_index\_of\_type}, enable type-based element access for types that occur exactly once in the tuple. This guarantees type-safe retrieval while all computations occur at compile-time.

Line~580--658:
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept {
  return t.template get<I>();
}

template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept {
  return std::move(t).template get<I>();
}

template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept {
  return t.template get<I>();
}

template <std::size_t I, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept {
  return std::move(t).template get<I>();
}

template <class T, class... Types> struct _count_of_type;

template <class T>
struct _count_of_type<T> : std::integral_constant<std::size_t, 0> {};

template <class T, class Head, class... Tail>
struct _count_of_type<T, Head, Tail...>
    : std::integral_constant<std::size_t,
                             (std::is_same_v<T, Head> ? 1 : 0) +
                                 _count_of_type<T, Tail...>::value> {};

template <class T, class... Types>
inline constexpr std::size_t _count_of_type_v =
    _count_of_type<T, Types...>::value;

template <class T, class... Types> struct _index_of_type;

template <class T, class... Tail>
struct _index_of_type<T, T, Tail...> : std::integral_constant<std::size_t, 0> {
};

template <class T, class Head, class... Tail>
struct _index_of_type<T, Head, Tail...>
    : std::integral_constant<std::size_t,
                             1 + _index_of_type<T, Tail...>::value> {};

template <class T> struct _index_of_type<T> {};

template <class T, class... Types>
inline constexpr std::size_t _index_of_type_v =
    _index_of_type<T, Types...>::value;

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(mystd::tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(t);
}

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(mystd::tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(std::move(t));
}

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const mystd::tuple<Types...> &t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(t);
}

template <class T, class... Types>
constexpr decltype(auto) get(const mystd::tuple<Types...> &&t) noexcept
  requires(_count_of_type_v<T, Types...> == 1)
{
  return get<_index_of_type_v<T, Types...>>(std::move(t));
}
\end{lstlisting}
\eit
\ssc{2-D-1-1 演算法設計}
\label{2-D-1-1}
程式執⾏效率相關請參見 \hyperref[2-D-1-2]{\textbf{2-D-1-2 程式執⾏效率優化}}；指標相關請參見 \hyperref[2-B-1-2]{\textbf{2-B-1-2 指標成員處理}} 中之各 \textbf{描述}；依照 STL C++20 標準實作的部分及其優化與巧思請參見本報告各章節與程式碼檔案；以下僅就Heap 與 priority\_queue 資料結構與演算法及Quick sort 演算法進行描述。
\sssc{Heap 與 priority\_queue 資料結構與演算法}
Heap 是一種以完全二元樹為邏輯模型、並以連續儲存空間實作的資料結構，常用於需要快速取得最大或最小元素的情境，如優先佇列（\texttt{priority\_queue}）。本實作以隨機存取疊代器（\texttt{random\_access\_iterator}）為基礎，提供一組符合 C++20 標準的 heap 演算法於 \verb|include/algorithm-heap.hpp| 中，又以 \verb|mystd::vector| 為預設底層容器，提供符合 C++20 標準的 \texttt{mystd::priority\_queue} container adapter 於 \verb|include/priority_queue.hpp| 中。

在結構表示上，heap 以陣列形式儲存元素。對於索引為 $i$ 的節點，其父節點索引為
\[\left\lfloor \frac{i-1}{2} \right\rfloor,\]
左右子節點索引分別為 $2i+1$ 與 $2i+2$。本實作預設以 \texttt{std::less<>} 建立最大堆（max-heap），並提供接受比較子（\texttt{Compare}）的多載版本，使 heap 的排序準則可完全由使用者自訂。

\bit
\item\texttt{push\_heap}：用於在既有 heap 的尾端插入一個新元素後，恢復 heap 性質。實作上，新元素位於最後一個索引，演算法透過「向上調整」（sift-up / bubble-up），反覆與其父節點比較；若新元素依比較子具有更高優先序，則與父節點交換，直到抵達根節點或不再違反 heap 性質為止。其時間複雜度為 $O(\log n)$。
\item\texttt{pop\_heap}：用於移除 heap 的堆頂元素。實作上，先將根節點與尾端元素交換，使原本的最大（或最小）元素被移動至尾端；接著對新的根節點執行向下調整（heapify-down），在左右子節點中選擇優先序較高者進行交換，直到 heap 性質恢復。其時間複雜度為 $O(\log n)$。
\item\texttt{make\_heap}：用於將任意排列的元素區間轉換為合法 heap。本實作採用自底向上的 heapify 策略，從最後一個非葉節點（索引 $\lfloor n/2 \rfloor - 1$）開始，依序對每個節點進行向下調整。相較於逐一插入並呼叫 \texttt{push\_heap} 的 $O(n\log n)$ 總時間複雜度，此方法的時間複雜度為 $O(n)$，為建構 heap 的最佳解。此特性在 \texttt{priority\_queue} 的建構子中尤為重要，能有效降低由大量初始資料建立優先佇列的成本。
\item\texttt{sort\_heap}：假設輸入區間已滿足 heap 性質，透過反覆呼叫 \texttt{pop\_heap}，將目前堆頂元素移至區間尾端，並逐步縮小 heap 範圍，最終得到一個依比較子排序完成的序列。其時間複雜度為 $O(n \log n)$，屬於不需額外記憶體的原地排序（in-place sort），但不具穩定性。
\item\texttt{is\_heap} 用於檢查一個區間是否滿足 heap 性質。實作上，對每一個父節點檢查其與左右子節點之間是否符合比較子所定義的順序關係，最壞情況需檢查所有內部節點，時間複雜度為 $O(n)$。
\item\texttt{is\_heap\_until} 則在檢查過程中，一旦發現第一個違反 heap 性質的子節點，立即回傳其疊代器位置，否則回傳 \texttt{last}。
\eit

\texttt{mystd::priority\_queue} 內部以一個隨機存取容器（預設為 \texttt{mystd::vector}）作為底層儲存結構，並完全透過上述 heap 演算法維護其不變量：
\bit
\item 在所有建構子中，當底層容器含有初始元素時，皆呼叫 \texttt{make\_heap} 以確保正確初始化。
\item \texttt{push} 與 \texttt{emplace} 透過 \texttt{push\_heap} 在插入後恢復 heap 性質。
\item \texttt{pop} 則以 \texttt{pop\_heap} 搭配容器尾端刪除完成移除操作。
\item \texttt{top} 則直接回傳根節點，時間複雜度為 $O(1)$。
\eit

綜上所述，本實作將 heap 的所有核心操作以泛型演算法形式獨立實現，並配合 Concepts 與比較子設計，再由 \texttt{priority\_queue} 組合使用，清楚區分資料結構介面與演算法細節，並確保符合 C++20 標準。
\sssc{Quick sort 演算法}
Quick sort（快速排序）是一種基於「分割（partition）」與「分治（divide and conquer）」策略的比較式排序演算法。我在 \verb|include/qsort.hpp| 的實作中以隨機存取疊代器（\texttt{random\_access\_iterator}）為前提，並透過 Concepts（\texttt{std::sortable}）在編譯期保證元素可比較與可交換，設計目標在於語意清楚、實作精簡，並與 C++ 標準庫風格一致。

Quick sort 的核心流程可分為三個步驟：
\begin{enumerate}
  \item 選擇一個樞紐元素（pivot）。
  \item 對區間進行分割，使所有小於 pivot 的元素位於其左側，大於等於 pivot 的元素位於其右側。
  \item 對左右兩個子區間遞迴套用相同的排序流程。
\end{enumerate}

在本實作中，pivot 固定選擇為區間尾端元素（\texttt{*(last - 1)}），以降低實作複雜度並避免額外儲存空間。

分割階段使用兩個疊代器：
\begin{itemize}
  \item \texttt{i}：指向目前「小於 pivot 區間」的尾端。
  \item \texttt{j}：由 \texttt{first} 走訪至 \texttt{last - 1}，逐一檢查元素。
\end{itemize}

對於每一個 \texttt{*j}：
\begin{itemize}
  \item 若 \texttt{*j < pivot}（或使用比較子 \texttt{comp(*j, pivot)}），則將 \texttt{*j} 與 \texttt{*i} 交換，並將 \texttt{i} 前進一格。
\end{itemize}

當走訪完成後，\texttt{i} 所指的位置即為 pivot 的最終正確位置，透過將 \texttt{*i} 與 pivot 交換，使得：
\[[\text{first}, i) < \text{pivot}, \quad *i = \text{pivot}, \quad (i, \text{last}) \ge \text{pivot}.\]

完成分割後，演算法遞迴處理：
\begin{itemize}
  \item 左子區間：\texttt{[first, i)}
  \item 右子區間：\texttt{[i + 1, last)}
\end{itemize}

遞迴終止條件為區間長度小於等於 1，此時區間已自然有序。

第二個多載版本接受使用者自訂的比較子 \texttt{Compare comp}，所有原本以 \texttt{<} 判斷的地方，皆改為 \texttt{comp(a, b)}。此設計與 \texttt{std::sort} 的介面設計保持一致。

\textbf{時間複雜度}：
\begin{itemize}
  \item 平均時間複雜度：$O(n \log n)$：遞迴深度 $O(\log n)$，每一層分割成本 $O(n)$。
  \item 最壞時間複雜度：$O(n^2)$：當 pivot 選擇不佳（例如固定選尾端），遞迴深度可能退化為 $n$。
\end{itemize}

\textbf{演算法特性}：
\begin{itemize}
  \item 原地排序（in-place sort）：僅使用遞迴呼叫堆疊，不需額外輔助陣列。
  \item 非穩定排序：相等元素在排序後的相對順序不保證維持。
  \item Pivot 選擇策略簡單：本實作未引入 median-of-three 或隨機化 pivot，故在理論最壞情況下可能退化。
\end{itemize}

程式碼如下：（line~9--39）
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
template<std::random_access_iterator RandomIt>
requires std::sortable<RandomIt>
constexpr void qsort(RandomIt first, RandomIt last) {
    if (first >= last || std::distance(first, last) <= 1) return;
    RandomIt i = first;
    for (RandomIt j=first; j<last-1; j++) {
        if (*j < *(last - 1)) {
          mystd::swap(*i, *j);
          ++i;
        }
    }
    mystd::swap(*i, *(last - 1));
    qsort(first, i);
    qsort(i+1, last);
}

template<std::random_access_iterator RandomIt, class Compare>
requires std::sortable<RandomIt, Compare>
constexpr void qsort(RandomIt first, RandomIt last, Compare comp) {
    if (first >= last || std::distance(first, last) <= 1) return;
    RandomIt i = first;
    for (RandomIt j=first; j<last-1; j++) {
        if (comp(*j, *(last - 1))) {
          mystd::swap(*i, *j);
          ++i;
        }
    }
    mystd::swap(*i, *(last - 1));
    qsort(first, i, comp);
    qsort(i+1, last, comp);
}
\end{lstlisting}
\ssc{2-D-1-2 程式執⾏效率優化}
\label{2-D-1-2}
下針對我使用的各程式執⾏效率優化的技巧先闡述概念與有無使用的差異再舉出，再指出在本專案之用途。
\sssc{Compile-time branching with if constexpr in pointer and iterator operations}
\label{branching}
The \texttt{if constexpr} statement allows compile-time branching based on type traits or constant expressions. Unlike a regular \texttt{if}, branches that evaluate to \texttt{false} are discarded during compilation, so no code is generated for them. This feature increases efficiency in pointer and iterator operations in several ways:

\begin{itemize}
  \item \textbf{Elimination of runtime checks:} Operations such as \texttt{allocate}, \texttt{construct}, or \texttt{destroy} can adapt to whether an allocator provides a specific interface without incurring runtime conditional checks.
  \item \textbf{Faster paths for specific scenarios:} Optimized paths can be implemented for particular cases, such as trivially copyable elements, forward iterators, or contiguous iterators.
  \item \textbf{Optimized code paths:} Only the necessary branch is compiled, allowing the compiler to produce specialized, streamlined machine code for each type or iterator category.
  \item \textbf{Enabling inlining and further compile-time optimizations:} With \texttt{if constexpr}, the compiler sees a fully resolved control flow, enabling aggressive inlining and constant propagation.
  \item \textbf{Reduced template bloat and branching overhead:} Generic containers and iterators can handle multiple scenarios (e.g., const vs. non-const access, random access vs. circular access) without runtime penalties.
\end{itemize}

Many examples are demonstrated in \textbf{2-B-1-2 指標成員處理} 中的 \hyperref[vector-list]{\textbf{include/vector.hpp}} and described in its \hyperref[vector-describe]{\textbf{描述}}.
\sssc{constexpr function}
\label{constexpr}
The constexpr specifier is introduced in C++11, and declares that it is possible to evaluate the value of the entities at compile time. Such entities can then be used where only compile time constant expressions are allowed (provided that appropriate function arguments are given).

Since C++20, many functions in STL is constexpr, notably many of the constructors and member functions of most containers. The list below is the specification of constexpr function in C++20, the standard my implementation complies with.
\bit
\item A constexpr specifier used in the first declaration of a function or static data member implies inline. If any declaration of a function or function template has a constexpr specifier, then every declaration must contain that specifier.
\item A function or function template can be declared constexpr. A function is constexpr-suitable if all following conditions are satisfied:
\bit
\item If it is a constructor or destructor, its class does not have any virtual base class.
\item Its return type (if exists) is a literal type.
\item Each of its parameter types is a literal type.
\item It is not a coroutine.
\item Its function body is = default, = delete, or does not enclose the following:
\bit
\item goto statements
\item statements with labels other than case and default
\item definitions of variables of non-literal types
\item definitions of variables of static or thread storage duration
\eit
\eit
\item Except for instantiated constexpr functions, non-templated constexpr functions must be constexpr-suitable.
\item For a non-constructor constexpr function that is neither defaulted nor templated, if no argument values exist such that an invocation of the function could be an evaluated subexpression of a core constant expression, the program is ill-formed, no diagnostic required.
\item For a templated constexpr function, if no specialization of the function/class template would make the templated function constexpr-suitable when considered as a non-templated function, the program is ill-formed, no diagnostic required.
\item An invocation of a constexpr function in a given context produces the same result as an invocation of an equivalent non-constexpr function in the same context in all respects, with the following exceptions:
\bit
\item An invocation of a constexpr function can appear in a constant expression.
\item Copy elision is not performed in a constant expression.
\eit
\item constexpr constructor: On top of the requirements of constexpr functions, a constructor also needs to satisfy all following conditions to be constexpr-suitable:
\bit
\item Its function body is = delete or satisfies the following additional requirements:
\bit
\item Every non-variant non-static data member and base class subobject is initialized.
\item If the constructor is a delegating constructor, the target constructor is a constexpr constructor.
\item If the constructor is a non-delegating constructor, every constructor selected to initialize non-static data members and base class subobjects is a constexpr constructor.
\eit
\item The class does not have any virtual base class.
\eit
For a constexpr constructor that is neither defaulted nor templated, if no argument values exist such that an invocation of the function could be an evaluated subexpression of the initialization full-expression of some object subject to constant expression, the program is ill-formed, no diagnostic required.
\item constexpr destructor: On top of the requirements of constexpr functions, a destructor also needs to satisfy all following conditions to be constexpr-suitable:
\bit
\item For every subobject of class type or (possibly multi-dimensional) array thereof, that class type has a constexpr destructor.
\item The class does not have any virtual base class.
\eit
\eit
When a function is marked as \texttt{constexpr}, the compiler can evaluate its result during compilation if all arguments are known, producing a constant value in the generated code. This has several efficiency benefits:
\begin{itemize}
  \item \textbf{Reduced runtime overhead:} Computations are moved from execution time to compilation, eliminating repeated calculations during program execution.
  \item \textbf{Improved inlining opportunities:} Compile-time results can be directly substituted into expressions, reducing function call overhead and enabling further compiler optimizations.
  \item \textbf{Enabling compile-time checks:} Conditions such as array bounds, template arguments, or static assertions can be verified at compile time, avoiding runtime errors.
  \item \textbf{Optimized memory layout:} Constant expressions can be embedded directly in read-only memory or used to size arrays and other structures efficiently.
\end{itemize}
Many examples are shown in \textbf{2-B-1-2 指標成員處理} 的 \hyperref[vector-list]{\textbf{include/vector.hpp}}.
\sssc{Compile-time polymorphism-related optimization}
請參見 \hyperref[2-C-4-3]{\textbf{2-C-4-3 polymorphism 相關的 class 或 function 間的對應關係}}。
\sssc{Named Return Value Optimization (NRVO)}
Named Return Value Optimization (NRVO) is a compiler optimization that eliminates unnecessary copy or move constructions when returning a local object from a function.

If a function returns a named local variable matching the function's return type directly without parenthesis, the compiler is allowed to construct the object directly in the caller's storage, bypassing temporary objects.
\sssc{no\_unique\_address attribute}
Introduced in C++20, \texttt{[[no\_unique\_address]]} attribute allows empty member objects to be optimized similarly to empty bases, reducing storage overhead. It is used in \verb|include/vector.hpp| line~46:
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
  [[no_unique_address]] Allocator alloc;
\end{lstlisting}
\ssc{2-D-1-3 程式碼管理版本控制}
在本專案中，我們採用 \textbf{Git} 作為程式碼版本控制工具，並使用 \textbf{GitHub} 作為遠端託管平台，以支持多人協作與專案管理。Git 以其分散式版本控制的特性，允許每位開發者在本地完整保存整個程式碼庫，這不僅使得開發者能夠離線進行提交與檢查，也確保即便遠端倉庫出現問題，本地版本仍可完整恢復。GitHub 則提供了遠端集中管理、協作審核及歷史追蹤功能，讓專案能夠在多個開發者之間順利運作。

利用 Git 的分支（branch）機制，我們可以針對不同功能、修正或實驗性功能建立獨立分支。每位組員可在自己的分支上進行開發，彼此的修改互不干擾，並避免直接影響主分支（main）的穩定性。完成開發後，透過 merge 或 rebase 將功能分支合併至主分支，Git 會自動檢測修改衝突，並提供差異比較工具以協助解決。

Git 提供多種便利工具與指令以強化程式碼管理，例如：
\begin{itemize}
  \item \verb|git clone|：從遠端倉庫複製完整專案到本地，建立初始工作環境。
  \item \verb|git status|：顯示工作目錄與暫存區的狀態，檢查檔案是否被修改、暫存或尚未追蹤。
  \item \verb|git add|：將檔案變更加入暫存區，準備提交。
  \item \verb|git mv|：重新命名或移動檔案，Git 會正確追蹤檔案變更歷史。
  \item \verb|git rm|：刪除檔案並同步移出版本控制。
  \item \verb|git commit|：將暫存區內容提交至本地倉庫，形成可追蹤的版本紀錄。
  \item \verb|git diff|：比較不同提交、分支或檔案狀態的差異，協助檢查修改內容。
  \item \verb|git log|：檢視提交歷史、作者與提交訊息，便於回溯版本與審查變更。
  \item \verb|git grep|：在倉庫版本控制下的檔案中搜尋關鍵字，方便快速定位程式碼。
  \item \verb|git branch|：查看、建立或刪除分支，管理不同開發線路。
  \item \verb|git checkout|：切換分支或還原特定檔案至指定提交狀態。
  \item \verb|git merge|：將其他分支的修改合併到目前分支，可能需要處理衝突。
  \item \verb|git rebase|：將一個分支的提交重新套用到另一分支之上，使提交歷史保持線性。
  \item \verb|git stash|：暫存尚未提交的修改，清理工作目錄以便切換分支或進行其他操作。
  \item \verb|git reset|：重設 HEAD 或暫存區狀態，常用於取消暫存或回退提交（需謹慎使用）。
  \item \verb|git revert|：建立一個新的提交以反向還原指定提交，安全地修正已發布的錯誤。
  \item \verb|git cherry-pick|：選取特定提交套用到另一分支，常用於單一錯誤修正或功能移植。
  \item \verb|git tag|：為特定提交建立標籤，常用於版本發布與里程碑標記。
  \item \verb|git fetch|：從遠端倉庫取得最新提交資訊，但不自動合併。
  \item \verb|git pull|：從遠端取得最新提交並自動合併到目前分支。
  \item \verb|git push|：將本地提交推送至遠端倉庫，與團隊成員同步進度。
\end{itemize}

相較於傳統版本控制方式（如手動備份、單一中央儲存庫或共享網路磁碟），Git 的優勢十分明顯：
\begin{itemize}
  \item \textbf{高度分支靈活性}：允許多分支並行開發，減少程式碼覆寫與衝突機率。
  \item \textbf{完整歷史追蹤}：每次提交都包含作者、時間、修改內容，便於審查、回滾與責任追溯。
  \item \textbf{離線操作能力}：本地倉庫完整，開發者可離線編輯、提交與檢查程式碼，再於網路恢復時同步遠端。
  \item \textbf{協作效率高}：結合 GitHub，支援 pull request、code review 與 issue 管理，使多人協作更有條理。
  \item \textbf{衝突解決工具完善}：自動檢測 merge conflict，並提供比對與手動解決工具，降低人為錯誤。
\end{itemize}

在本專案中，我們也使用 GitHub CLI（\verb|gh|）進行 GitHub 操作，例如：
\begin{itemize}
  \item 建立、檢視及管理 pull request 和 issue。
  \item 透過命令列快速審核、合併分支以及發布 release。
  \item 自動化部分操作流程，提升團隊效率。
\end{itemize}

在團隊專案中，我負責教導組員如何使用 Git 與 GitHub CLI，包括：
\begin{itemize}
  \item 建立分支、切換分支、合併分支。
  \item 提交與推送程式碼，保持本地與遠端同步。
  \item 使用 pull request、issue、review 流程管理功能合併。
  \item 使用 \verb|git diff|、\verb|git log| 與 \verb|git status| 等進行程式碼檢查與追蹤修改。
\end{itemize}

此外，我也負責主要處理專案開發中最具挑戰性的部分——\textbf{merge conflict}。當多位組員在同一程式碼區塊進行修改時，Git 會自動標示衝突。我需要仔細分析各分支修改的意圖，判斷正確的合併方式，並手動解決衝突，以確保最終程式碼可以正常編譯與運行。在此過程中，我也與組員保持溝通，統一程式碼風格與命名規則，減少未來衝突發生的可能性。

另外，我負責撰寫 Linux 與 Windows 的 release scripts，根據老師要求將編譯完成的程式包裝為 zip 檔，並自動建立 GitHub release，以提供團隊與使用者下載最新穩定版本。

總結來說，透過 Git 與 GitHub 的版本控制與分支管理，我們的專案能夠在多人開發、頻繁修改與測試的情況下，保持程式碼的穩定性、完整性與可追溯性。這大幅提升了團隊的協作效率，降低了程式碼錯誤與重工風險，使整個開發流程更加順暢與可控。
\ssc{2-D-2-1 美⼯細節}
\label{2-D-2-1}
我所設計的美工部分細節如下：
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Tap notes}：使用 \href{https://gallery.yopriceville.com/Free-Clipart-Pictures/Ribbons-and-Banners-PNG/Decorative_Banner_Transparent_PNG_Picture}{網路圖片}。
\item \textbf{Hold notes}：使用 \href{https://www.pngall.com/rectangle-frame-png/download/176562/}{網路圖片}。
\item \textbf{Hold notes 長按變色}：此效果由我設計，程式碼節錄自 \verb|Renderer.hpp| 第 405~406 行：
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
float pulse = 0.7f + 0.3f * sin((float)holdPressedTime / 100.0f);
color = {0, static_cast<Uint8>(150 * pulse), 0, 255};
\end{lstlisting}
\item \textbf{遊戲中的計分與資訊文字}：由我設計。
\item \textbf{各 lane 特效}：基於 \href{https://anubis.techaro.lol/}{Anubis} 吉祥物。
\item \textbf{中央特效}：基於 \href{https://www.gnu.org/}{GNU} 與 \href{https://gcc.gnu.org/}{GCC} 吉祥物。
\item \textbf{設定頁面}：由我設計，程式碼節錄自 \verb|BeatRunner.cpp| 第 634~775 行：
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
void showSettings(SDL_Renderer *renderer, SDL_Window *window) {
  bool running = true;
  SDL_Event e;

  SDL_Color white = {255, 255, 255, 255};
  SDL_Color grey = {100, 100, 100, 255};
  SDL_Color blue = {0, 128, 255, 255};

  SDL_Rect lanesMinus = {310, 80, 40, 40};
  SDL_Rect lanesPlus = {410, 80, 40, 40};
  SDL_Rect fragmentsMinus = {310, 140, 40, 40};
  SDL_Rect fragmentsPlus = {410, 140, 40, 40};
  SDL_Rect modDropdown = {310, 200, 850, 40};
  SDL_Rect okButton = {SCREEN_WIDTH / 2 - 50, 280, 100, 50};

  std::vector<std::string> modKeys;
  for (auto &p : getModMap())
    modKeys.push_back(p.first);
  int selectedModIndex = 0;

  bool dropdownOpen = false;

  while (running) {
    while (SDL_PollEvent(&e)) {
      if (e.type == SDL_QUIT ||
          (e.type == SDL_KEYDOWN && !e.key.repeat &&
           (e.key.keysym.mod & KMOD_CTRL) && e.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_w)) {
        destroyMainMenuTextures();
        delete chartParser;
        delete musicManager;
        SDL_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        SDL_DestroyWindow(window);
        TTF_CloseFont(large_font);
        TTF_CloseFont(medium_font);
        TTF_CloseFont(small_font);
        TTF_Quit();
        IMG_Quit();
        SDL_Quit();
        exit(0);
      }

      if (e.type == SDL_MOUSEBUTTONDOWN && e.button.button == SDL_BUTTON_LEFT) {
        int mx = e.button.x, my = e.button.y;
        if (pointInRect(mx, my, lanesMinus)) {
          if (LANES > 1)
            --LANES;
        } else if (pointInRect(mx, my, lanesPlus)) {
          if (LANES < 9)
            ++LANES;
        } else if (pointInRect(mx, my, fragmentsMinus)) {
          if (FRAGMENTS > 2)
            --FRAGMENTS;
        } else if (pointInRect(mx, my, fragmentsPlus)) {
          if (FRAGMENTS < 100)
            ++FRAGMENTS;
        } else if (pointInRect(mx, my, modDropdown)) {
          dropdownOpen = !dropdownOpen;
        } else if (pointInRect(mx, my, okButton)) {
          running = false;
        }

        if (dropdownOpen) {
          for (int i = 0; i < (int)modKeys.size(); ++i) {
            SDL_Rect itemRect = {modDropdown.x, modDropdown.y + 40 * (i + 1),
                                 modDropdown.w, 40};
            if (pointInRect(mx, my, itemRect)) {
              selectedModIndex = i;
              MOD = modKeys[i];
              dropdownOpen = false;
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

    SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 0, 0, 0, 255);
    SDL_RenderClear(renderer);

    renderRoundedRect(renderer, lanesMinus, 10, blue);
    renderRoundedRect(renderer, lanesPlus, 10, blue);
    renderRoundedRect(renderer, fragmentsMinus, 10, blue);
    renderRoundedRect(renderer, fragmentsPlus, 10, blue);
    renderRoundedRect(renderer, modDropdown, 10, grey);
    renderRoundedRect(renderer, okButton, 15, blue);

    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "LANES:", 50, 100, white, ALIGN_LEFT);
    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "FRAGMENTS:", 50, 160, white, ALIGN_LEFT);
    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "MOD:", 50, 220, white, ALIGN_LEFT);

    renderText(renderer, medium_font, std::to_string(LANES), 380, 105, white);
    renderText(renderer, medium_font, std::to_string(FRAGMENTS), 380, 165,
               white);
    renderText(renderer, small_font, MOD, 330, 220, white, ALIGN_LEFT);

    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "-", lanesMinus.x + 20, lanesMinus.y + 20,
               white);
    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "+", lanesPlus.x + 20, lanesPlus.y + 20,
               white);
    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "-", fragmentsMinus.x + 20,
               fragmentsMinus.y + 20, white);
    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "+", fragmentsPlus.x + 20,
               fragmentsPlus.y + 20, white);
    renderText(renderer, medium_font, "OK", okButton.x + 49, okButton.y + 27,
               white);

    if (dropdownOpen) {
      for (int i = 0; i < (int)modKeys.size(); ++i) {
        SDL_Rect itemRect = {modDropdown.x, modDropdown.y + 40 * (i + 1),
                             modDropdown.w, 40};
        renderText(renderer, small_font, modKeys[i], itemRect.x + 10,
                   itemRect.y, white, ALIGN_LEFT);
      }
    }

    SDL_RenderPresent(renderer);
  }

  if (chartParser->load(selectedChartPath)) {
    // std::cout << "[OK] Chart loaded successfully: " << selectedChartPath <<
    // std::endl;
    mouseNotesPtr = &chartParser->getMouseNotes();
    musicManager->loadMusic(chartParser->getMusicFile());
  } else {
    std::cerr << "[ERROR] Failed to load chart" << std::endl;
  }

  exactFragmentMs = 60000.0f / (double)chartParser->getBPM() /
                    (double)chartParser->getFragmentsPerBeat();
  MS_PER_FRAGMENT = (uint32_t)exactFragmentMs;
  if (game)
    delete game;
  game = new Game(LANES, FRAGMENTS, MS_PER_FRAGMENT, keyNotes);
  if (gameRenderer)
    delete gameRenderer;
  gameRenderer = new Renderer(*game, SCREEN_WIDTH, SCREEN_HEIGHT, renderer,
                              large_font, medium_font, small_font);

  SettingsFunc modSettingsFuncLocal = mystd::get<2>(getModMap()[MOD]);
  if (modSettingsFuncLocal) {
    modSettingsFuncLocal(renderer, small_font, SCREEN_WIDTH, SCREEN_HEIGHT);
  }
}
\end{lstlisting}
\item \textbf{康威生命遊戲模組設定頁面}：由我設計，程式碼節錄自 \verb|BeatRunner.cpp| 第 103~253 行：
\begin{lstlisting}[language=C++]
void gameOfLifeSettings(SDL_Renderer *renderer, TTF_Font *font, int screenWidth,
                        int screenHeight) {
  mystd::array<uint16_t, 2> tempRules = currentRules;

  const int buttonSize = 40;
  const int buttonSpacing = 5;
  const int rowSpacing = 60;

  int totalWidth = 9 * buttonSize + 8 * buttonSpacing;
  int startX = (screenWidth - totalWidth) / 2;
  int row1Y = screenHeight / 2 - rowSpacing;
  int row2Y = screenHeight / 2 + rowSpacing;

  const int okButtonWidth = 100;
  const int okButtonHeight = 50;
  int okButtonX = (screenWidth - okButtonWidth) / 2;
  int okButtonY = row2Y + rowSpacing * 2;

  bool settingsRunning = true;
  bool redrawNeeded = true;

  while (settingsRunning) {
    SDL_Event event;
    while (SDL_PollEvent(&event)) {
      if (event.type == SDL_QUIT) {
        settingsRunning = false;
        break;
      } else if (event.type == SDL_KEYDOWN) {
        if (event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_RETURN ||
            event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_ESCAPE) {
          currentRules = tempRules;
          settingsRunning = false;
        }
      } else if (event.type == SDL_MOUSEBUTTONDOWN) {
        if (event.button.button == SDL_BUTTON_LEFT) {
          int mouseX = event.button.x;
          int mouseY = event.button.y;

          for (int i = 0; i < 9; ++i) {
            int buttonX = startX + i * (buttonSize + buttonSpacing);
            SDL_Rect buttonRect = {buttonX, row1Y, buttonSize, buttonSize};

            if (mouseX >= buttonRect.x &&
                mouseX <= buttonRect.x + buttonRect.w &&
                mouseY >= buttonRect.y &&
                mouseY <= buttonRect.y + buttonRect.h) {
              tempRules[0] ^= (1 << i);
              redrawNeeded = true;
            }
          }

          for (int i = 0; i < 9; ++i) {
            int buttonX = startX + i * (buttonSize + buttonSpacing);
            SDL_Rect buttonRect = {buttonX, row2Y, buttonSize, buttonSize};

            if (mouseX >= buttonRect.x &&
                mouseX <= buttonRect.x + buttonRect.w &&
                mouseY >= buttonRect.y &&
                mouseY <= buttonRect.y + buttonRect.h) {
              tempRules[1] ^= (1 << i);
              redrawNeeded = true;
            }
          }

          SDL_Rect okRect = {okButtonX, okButtonY, okButtonWidth,
                             okButtonHeight};
          if (mouseX >= okRect.x && mouseX <= okRect.x + okRect.w &&
              mouseY >= okRect.y && mouseY <= okRect.y + okRect.h) {
            currentRules = tempRules;
            settingsRunning = false;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (redrawNeeded) {
      SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 30, 30, 40, 255);
      SDL_RenderClear(renderer);

      for (int i = 0; i < 9; ++i) {
        int buttonX = startX + i * (buttonSize + buttonSpacing);
        SDL_Rect buttonRect = {buttonX, row1Y, buttonSize, buttonSize};

        bool enabled = (tempRules[0] >> i) & 0b1;

        if (enabled) {
          SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 100, 200, 100, 255);
        } else {
          SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 200, 100, 100, 255);
        }
        SDL_RenderFillRect(renderer, &buttonRect);

        SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 255, 255, 255, 255);
        SDL_RenderDrawRect(renderer, &buttonRect);

        SDL_Color numColor = {255, 255, 255, 255};
        renderText(renderer, std::to_string(i), buttonX + buttonSize / 2,
                   row1Y + buttonSize / 2, font, numColor, ALIGN_CENTER);
      }

      for (int i = 0; i < 9; ++i) {
        int buttonX = startX + i * (buttonSize + buttonSpacing);
        SDL_Rect buttonRect = {buttonX, row2Y, buttonSize, buttonSize};

        bool enabled = (tempRules[1] >> i) & 0b1;

        if (enabled) {
          SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 100, 200, 100, 255);
        } else {
          SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 200, 100, 100, 255);
        }
        SDL_RenderFillRect(renderer, &buttonRect);

        SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 255, 255, 255, 255);
        SDL_RenderDrawRect(renderer, &buttonRect);
        SDL_Color numColor = {255, 255, 255, 255};
        renderText(renderer, std::to_string(i), buttonX + buttonSize / 2,
                   row2Y + buttonSize / 2, font, numColor, ALIGN_CENTER);
      }

      SDL_Rect okRect = {okButtonX, okButtonY, okButtonWidth, okButtonHeight};
      SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 100, 150, 255, 255);
      SDL_RenderFillRect(renderer, &okRect);
      SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(renderer, 255, 255, 255, 255);
      SDL_RenderDrawRect(renderer, &okRect);

      SDL_Color textColor = {255, 255, 255, 255};
      std::string surviveText = "Survive with neighbors:";
      std::string reviveText = "Revive with neighbors:";

      int surviveTextX = screenWidth / 2;
      int surviveTextY = row1Y - 40;
      renderText(renderer, surviveText, surviveTextX, surviveTextY, font,
                 textColor, ALIGN_CENTER);

      int reviveTextX = screenWidth / 2;
      int reviveTextY = row2Y - 40;
      renderText(renderer, reviveText, reviveTextX, reviveTextY, font,
                 textColor, ALIGN_CENTER);

      std::string okText = "OK";
      int okTextX = okButtonX + okButtonWidth / 2;
      int okTextY = okButtonY + okButtonHeight / 2;
      renderText(renderer, okText, okTextX, okTextY, font, textColor,
                 ALIGN_CENTER);

      SDL_RenderPresent(renderer);
      redrawNeeded = false;
    }
  }
}
\end{lstlisting}
\item \textbf{倒數動畫}：GO 頁面的圖片使用 \href{https://go.dev/}{The Go Programming Language} 吉祥物，其餘部分由我設計。
\end{itemize}
